 har maheene skool main dril hoti he

 ek naagarik samaaj ke taur par bharatiyon kaa vyavhaar japani logon se kis tarah alag hota he
 What is the Japanese system
 is par bhi baat prime time main
 The death toll due to earthquake in Nepal has increased to more than 3700
 abhi tak 6500 se zyada ghayalon kaa pataa chalaa he
 2500 Indians have been evacuated from there
 bharat ne 285 sadasyon kii team bheji he jinamein doctor or paramedics hai
 The NDRF has said that 10 teams are already engaged in relief and rescue work there, but to speed it up, six more teams are being sent
 vayusena ke das helicopter bhi kathmandu or pokhada ke upar raahat or bachaav ke liye udaan bhar rahe hai
 
 
 The Indian team is engaged in rescue and relief operations on a war footing
 centre sarkaar lagaataar sari gatividhiyon ko monitor kar rahi he
 Voluntary organizations have also become active with the government
 twitor par kai logon ne thank you piem kaa hashtag bhi chalaaya or piem modi ne bhi kaha ki shukriya sena or hamaari seva bhav kii parampara kaa

 china ne bhi 62 sadasyon kii ek search team bheji he
 China has also sent emergency tents, generators and blanket clothes
 china ne 30 lakh dollar kii madad raashi dene kii ghoshnaa kii he
 Israel has also sent a team of 260 members consisting of 122 doctors, nurses and paramedics
 iske alaava pakistan, britain, bhutan, japan, singapore malaysia kai chote bade desh nepal kii madad ke liye aage aae hai

 bharat main bhi 72 logon kii bukamp se maut hui he

 bukamp kab aayega ye koi nahin bataa saktaa lekin himalay ke ilaake main bukamp aayega yah sabko pataa he
 According to scientists, about 500 million years ago, the Earth was divided into two large continents
 
 
 uresia or gondvanaa land
 In the course of development of the earth, Gondwana land broke into many pieces and moved towards different directions
 iskaa ek hissaa jo bhartiya upmahadweep bana wo urasian plate se takaraayaa
 The folds formed by the same bump and rub between the two plates form the Himalayas
 bhartiya plate aaj bhi paanch centimetre prati varsh kii dar se urasian plate par dabaav bana rahi he, yaa kahen ki uske neeche khisak rahi he
 Earthquakes occur here when the energy released between the two plates is released while staying under the hidden energy
 is himalayan ilaake main aath kii tivrata ke aasapaas ke bukamp aate rahe hai
 Such as Kangra in 1905, bihar-nepal border in 1934, Shillong in 1897 and Assam in 1950
 lekin is graphix main jo aap laal lakeer dekh rahe hai vahaan aath kii tivrata kaa bukamp beete qareeb do sau saal main nahin aayaa he
 a recent earthquake has occurred at the eastern end of this line
 bhuvaigyanikon ke mutabik is laal lakeer jise central sizmik gap kehete hai us par bada bukamp aane kii ashanka lagaataar bani hui he kyonki yahaan zamin ke neeche kaafii dabaav bana hua he or isaki urja kabhi bhi kisi bukamp kii shakl le sakati he
 a large part of India is covered by this red streak, ie the Central Scientific Gap
 himalay kaa ilaaka to sakriy zone he lekin gondvanaa to saath karod saal purana he, jo duniya kaa sabase sthir or sthaayee bhukhand he vahaan bhi bhuncup aa gaya
 The earthquakes in Koyna and Latur in Maharashtra shocked everyone
 philhal himalay or uresia plate kii dhakka mukki main ham sabaki jaan ataki hui he
 The house of our dreams hangs
 har bukamp ke baad ham sab apane hi ghar main beghar mahasoos karne lagate hai

 The area where your anchor lives and another panelist of today does not know who trusts
 pichley do dinon se jis kisi ko dekh rahaa hum wo apane flats ko shaq kii nazar se dekh rahaa he
 Experts say that if an earthquake strikes, it should be seated at the corner of walls inside the house
 sar jhukaa liya jaae or mumkin ho to kisi chiz se dhank liya jaae

 Eurasia and Gondwana Land
 dharti ke vikaas kram main gondvanaa land kai tukdon main tuutakar alag-alag dishaao kii ore badha
 a part of it which became the Indian subcontinent collided with the Eurasian Plate
 donon platon ke bich isi takkar or ragad se bani silavaton se himalay bana he
 The Indian plate is still under pressure on the Eurasian plate at the rate of five centimeters per year, or rather, sliding under it
 donon platon ke bich bad rahe is dabaav main chuphi urja rah rahakar jab release hoti he to yahaan bukamp aate hai
 There have been earthquakes of around eight magnitude in this Himalayan region
 jaise 1905 main kangra, 1934 main bihar-nepal border, 1897 main shilong or 1950 main assam
 But the red streak that you are seeing in this graphics, there has not been an earthquake of magnitude eight in the last two hundred years
 isi lakeer ke purvi chor par haal main bukamp aayaa he
 According to geologists, this red streak, called the Central Psychological Gap, is prone to a large earthquake because there is a lot of pressure below the ground and its energy can take the shape of an earthquake at any time
 is laal lakeer yani central sizmik gap se hindustan kaa bada hissaa laga hua he
 The Himalayan region is an active zone, but Gondwana is six hundred million years old, which is the most stable and permanent land plot in the world
 maharashtra ke koyna or latur main aaye bukamp ne sabko chaunkaa diya tha
 At present, all of us are stuck in the Himalayan and Eurasia Plate push
 hamaare sapanom kaa makaan lataka hua he
 After every earthquake, we all start feeling homeless in our own home
 jo ghar hamen mahfuz lagata he usee kii chat in dinon jaanaleva lag rahi he
 You have been reading in the newspapers for the last two-three days that large parts of eastern to north India are divided into seismic zones four and five
 jahaan aapkaa ye ankar rahata he or aaj ke ek or penlist rahete hai wo ilaaka to pataa nahin kiske bharose he
 For the last two days, whoever i am looking at, is looking at his flat with suspicion
 export bataate hai ki bukamp aane par ghar ke bheetar deevaaron ke kone par baith jaaya jaae
 The head is bowed and if possible be covered with something
 teble ke neeche baithne kii bhi raay di jaati lekin jab apane teble ko dekha to laga ki mushkil se ye crockeri kii nazaakat sambhaal paata he kancreet se to or dab jayega
 So leaving the corner and the table, your anchor ran towards the elevator, when he realized that the lift was dangerous, he started descending the stairs
 do baar yah galati doharaai
 i was not alone when i came out
 meri hi tarah zyaadaatar logon ne saim harakat kii thi
 The comments agar yah bukamp prabhavit ilaaka he to hamen baar-baar shikshit hone kii zarurat he
 It is not just about tall buildings, whether the street locality and shop buildings are safe or not, whether it is built on the basis of any guideline or not, it is a constant need to know and see
